Senior HR Executive

Responsibilities:

1. HR Operations & Administration - Manage end-to-end recruitment and onboarding for technical and non-technical roles - Maintain accurate employee records and manage the HRMS. - Track attendance, leave, and shift compliance, and coordinate payroll inputs. - Ensure statutory and legal compliance with PF, ESI, Shops & Establishments Act, etc. - Prepare HR letters, reports, and documents for internal and audit purposes.

2. Employee Engagement & Communication - Organize monthly engagement activities, recognition programs, and team-building events. - Conduct employee onboarding, induction, and periodic feedback sessions. - Act as a point of contact for employee queries, grievances, and HR support.

3. Performance Management Support - Assist in quarterly and annual appraisal processes and maintain performance data. - Schedule feedback sessions and help managers with documentation and communication. - Support HR in implementing PIP (Performance Improvement Plan) documentation and tracking.

  • Bachelor’s degree in HR, Business Administration, or related field (MBA in HR preferred).
  • 4-6 years of experience in an HR generalist role.
  • Prior experience in the IT/ITeS industry is highly preferred.
  • Proficient in MS Office and HRMS tools; knowledge of Canva or social media tools is a plus.
  • Strong communication skills (written & verbal) and high emotional intelligence.
  • Ability to multitask and thrive in a fast-paced, high-growth environment.

Apply by: 08 Dec 2025

Senior DevSecOps Engineer

We are looking for a Senior DevSecOps Engineer who will lead our cybersecurity, infrastructure automation, and DevSecOps practices as we transition into a secure, scalable, and modern engineering environment. This role is responsible for strengthening 2Base’s security posture, modernizing our pipelines, and guiding the team towards a secure-by-design culture. You will work closely with engineering, product, and leadership teams to ensure that our systems, applications, and cloud environments are secure, reliable, and future-ready.

Key Responsibilities

  • Define, implement, and enforce security standards, policies, and best practices across cloud and on-prem environments.
  • Conduct security risk assessments, perform vulnerability scans, coordinate penetration testing activities, and execute mitigation plans.
  • Architect, maintain, and enhance secure CI/CD pipelines with automated compliance and governance checkpoints.
  • Promote and uphold a strong “Security First” culture across engineering, ensuring secure design and development practices
  • Continuously monitor, detect, investigate, and respond to security threats, incidents, breaches, and anomalies.
  • Develop, own, and mature Infrastructure-as-Code practices using Terraform, Ansible, and other automation frameworks.
  • Design and lead secure cloud architectures across AWS, Azure, or GCP to support scalable and compliant deployments.
  • Build, operate, and secure containerized environments using Docker and Kubernetes with enforced security baselines.
  • Implement and maintain secure monitoring, logging, SIEM, and alerting systems for infrastructure and application layers.
  • Improve and optimize system reliability, scalability, performance, and fault tolerance across all critical workloads.
  • Mentor, guide, and upskill DevOps engineers in secure development, automation, and operational excellence.
  • Lead technical strategy, decision-making, tool selection, process improvements, and DevSecOps roadmap execution.
  • Collaborate closely with BA, PM, and Engineering teams to ensure security, performance, and delivery objectives align with organisational goals.

Required Skills & Experience

  • 4–8 years of experience in DevOps, Cloud, or Infrastructure engineering with strong security exposure.
  • Hands-on experience with CI/CD tools such as Jenkins, GitLab CI, or GitHub Actions.
  • Strong expertise in AWS, Azure, or GCP cloud platforms with a focus on secure architecture.
  • Proficiency in Infrastructure-as-Code using Terraform, Ansible, or similar tools.
  • Experience securing and managing Docker and Kubernetes environments.
  • Strong understanding of networking technologies: LAN/WAN, firewalls, VPN, load balancers.
  • Knowledge of security frameworks and standards (OWASP, NIST, CIS Benchmarks).
  • Experience with monitoring and logging tools (Prometheus, Grafana, ELK, CloudWatch, SIEM solutions).
  • Strong scripting skills (Python, Bash, Shell).
  • Excellent troubleshooting, analytical, and problem-solving skills.
  • Strong communication and collaboration skills with the ability to influence engineering teams.

Preferred Qualifications (Good to Have)

  • Diploma / Degree / B.Tech in IT, CS, MCA
  • Experience in SOC operations or exposure to SIEM and SOAR tools.
  • Relevant certifications such as:
  • AWS Security / DevOps Engineer – Professional
  • Certified Kubernetes Security Specialist (CKS)
  • CEH, CompTIA Security+, or equivalent.

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Senior Business Analyst

2Base Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

Lead requirement workshops, translate business needs into functional logic, and ensure documentation clarity. Requires 4+ years of BA experience with strong system-level thinking and collaboration.

4+ YearsSaaSAPIBusiness Analysis
Apply by: 08 Dec 2025

Senior Business Analyst

Key Responsibilities

  • Lead requirement workshops, client calls, and discovery discussions to understand business needs clearly.
  • Ask deeper questions, challenge assumptions, and validate the true business intent behind every requirement.
  • Convert ambiguous client inputs into structured, logical, and actionable functional understanding.
  • Break large features into modules, workflows, components, and clear dependencies.
  • Build strong system-level understanding involving APIs, integrations, data flow, and backend considerations.
  • Translate business processes into functional logic that development teams can execute.
  • Decompose requirements into use-case flows, system behaviours, edge cases, alternate paths, validation rules, and dependencies.
  • Prepare high-quality documentation, including BRD, FRD, SRS, workflows, state diagrams, data-flow diagrams, API requirement specs, and acceptance criteria.
  • Ensure all documentation is clear, logical, structured, testable, and ready for developers and QA to use.
  • Collaborate closely with developers, architects, QA, and product owners to validate feasibility and align understanding.
  • Ensure QA teams can derive test cases effectively from your functional logic and acceptance criteria.
  • Communicate confidently with clients, handle requirement discussions smoothly, and clarify misunderstandings immediately.
  • Push back politely on unclear or changing requirements and ensure final decisions are documented properly.
  • Maintain requirement traceability throughout the lifecycle and ensure zero ambiguity during handover to development.
  • Own the entire requirement lifecycle from discovery to development readiness with high accountability.
  • Drive clarity across teams by ensuring every requirement is complete, validated, and logically consistent.

Requirements

Required Skills & Experience

  • Minimum 4+ years of core Business Analyst experience with strong analytical and system-level thinking.
  • Ability to break down complex requirements into clear components, workflows, and functional logic.
  • Excellent verbal and written communication with confidence in client interactions and clarifications.
  • Proven experience in preparing SRS, BRD, FRD, workflows, and acceptance criteria with high clarity.
  • Ability to challenge assumptions politely, ask the right questions, and ensure zero ambiguity.
  • Strong collaboration experience with development, QA, architects, and cross-functional teams.
  • Understanding of API behaviours, integrations, data flows, and multi-module system interactions.
  • Ability to run requirement discussions, workshops, and independently lead discovery sessions.
  • Exposure to SaaS, scalable products, automation, or AI-supported systems is an added advantage.
  • Demonstrated ownership of requirements end-to-end, ensuring developer-ready and testable outputs.
  • Not suitable for UI-only thinkers, passive communicators, template-based writers, or those relying on AI for answers.
  • Success is defined by clear, testable requirements, zero rework, strong cross-team alignment, and confident communication.
  • Candidates must align with 2Base’s structured thinking, clarity-driven culture, and transformation of the BA function.

Minimum Qualifications

  • Bachelor’s degree in Computer Science, Engineering, Business, or related field
  • 4 to 8 years of experience as a Business Analyst or Product Analyst
  • Experience in SaaS or scalable product environments
  • Exposure to AI/Automation, integrations, or multi-module systems
  • Ability to run independent client workshops
  • Must have independently handled requirement ownership for at least one full project lifecycle

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Contact Information

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at careers@2basetechnologies.com

  • Understanding of HTML & CSS is an advantage.
  • Strong sense of color theory, composition, visual hierarchy, and typography.
  • Ability to communicate design rationale clearly and confidently present creative decisions.
  • A proactive mindset with the ability to work independently, take initiative, and deliver results with minimal supervision.

He/She must be:

  1. Creative thinker, not just an executor
  2. Ownership-driven, proactive, and self-motivated
  3. Curious about trends, AI advancements, and new design possibilities
  4. Understands design as a balance between aesthetics, message, and business impact.

Infopark

Junior SRE needed for fintech platform resilience and fraud detection. Responsibilities include ensuring uptime, monitoring transactions, and mitigating risk in a fast-paced environment.

1-2 YearsDatadogSplunkLinux
Apply by: 10 Dec 2025

Junior Service Reliability Engineer

Location: [WFO - Kochi] Team: Engineering & Risk Operations

Role Summary

We are looking for a Junior Service Reliability Engineer to help ensure the resilience, performance, and integrity of our fintech platform. In this hybrid role, you will drive efforts to maintain service uptime, while also using data-driven analysis to detect, respond to, and mitigate fraudulent activities. You’ll work at the intersection of engineering, risk, and operations—ensuring both our systems and our customers remain protected. This is a high-impact position ideal for someone with 1-2 years of experience, who thrives in a fast-paced, mission-critical payments or fintech environment.

Key Responsibilities

Service Reliability Engineering - Ensure high availability and performance of our customer-facing services and payment systems. - Design and implement observability and alerting strategies using Datadog, PagerDuty, and custom dashboards. - Troubleshoot alerts/logs/db across infrastructure, applications, and APIs, and perform root cause analysis. - Define and manage SLIs/SLOs/SLAs to measure and improve system health. - Develop and maintain automation scripts and tools for system provisioning, health checks, and failovers. - Collaborate with development and infrastructure teams to ensure scalable, fault-tolerant designs.

Fraud Detection & Risk Monitoring - Leverage Splunk/Datadog, internal logs, and behavioral data to monitor suspicious transaction patterns in real-time. - Investigate alerts, anomalies, and user behaviors to detect fraud, abuse, or financial risk exposure. - Tune detection rules, triggers, and risk signals based on observed fraud trends. - Work closely with compliance, fraud operations, and customer support on case investigation and resolution. - Develop and maintain dashboards and reports on fraud KPIs, incident metrics, and operational trends. - Participate in cross-functional fraud response processes and post-incident reviews.

Required Qualifications

  • 1-2+ years of experience in a combined SRE, DevOps, fraud analyst, or security operations role.
  • Strong experience with monitoring and alerting tools: Datadog, PagerDuty, Splunk.
  • Proficiency with Linux, shell scripting, and infrastructure troubleshooting in cloud environments (AWS, GCP, or Azure).
  • Solid understanding of service observability, incident response, and CI/CD pipelines.
  • Experience with fraud detection workflows or risk monitoring in fintech, payments, or transaction-heavy systems.
  • Comfortable writing queries (SQL, Splunk SPL) and working with large volumes of log or event data.
  • Strong collaboration skills and the ability to communicate clearly with technical and non-technical stakeholders.

Nice to Have

  • Exposure to KYC/AML systems or fraud detection frameworks in regulated environments.
  • Familiarity with secure API architecture, authentication flows (OAuth2, JWT), and access control.
  • Knowledge of PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, ISO 8583 or other financial compliance frameworks.
  • Hands-on experience with rule engines or anomaly detection models.
  • Certifications like AWS DevOps Engineer, CFE (Certified Fraud Examiner), or similar.

What You’ll Get

  • A unique opportunity to work across both service reliability and fraud detection.
  • Impactful work supporting secure, high-volume payment operations.
  • A collaborative, data-driven culture with a strong engineering and risk mindset.
  • Career growth through ownership of complex systems and security initiatives.

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at lavanya.a@arttechgroup.com

Test Architect

Reflections Info Systems (P) Ltd
Technopark

Seeking an experienced Test Architect to define testing strategies for enterprise platforms. Responsibilities include ensuring quality across diverse systems and leading test automation efforts.

8+ YearsTest AutomationMicroservicesCI/CD
Apply by: 12 Dec 2025

Test Architect

Company: Reflections Info Systems (P) Ltd Location: 9A2, Carnival Technopark, Kariyavattom P.O, Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala, India, 695581 Website: http://www.reflectionsglobal.com Closing Date: 12, Dec 2025 Job Published: 05, Dec 2025 Contact Email: Careers@reflectionsinfos.com

Brief Description

We are looking for 8+ years experienced candidates for this role.

Description

The Test Architect is responsible for defining and governing the overall testing strategy, frameworks, and practices for mission-critical enterprise platforms running across multiple on-premises data centres and a DR site. This role ensures that functional, integration, regression, performance, security, GIS, and DR testing are designed and executed in a consistent, automated, and repeatable way across legacy and modernized components. The Test Architect works closely with application, integration, GIS, infrastructure, DevOps, and security teams to enable high-quality releases as the platform transitions from monolithic and legacy stacks to microservices, modern web UIs, and containerized workloads.

Responsibilities

  • Define the end-to-end test strategy and test architecture for a large, mission-critical platform, covering functional, integration, regression, system, UAT support, and non-functional testing (performance, reliability, security, usability).
  • Design a comprehensive test approach that supports coexistence of legacy and modernized components (web, desktop, mobile/MDT, APIs, GIS services), ensuring regression coverage across phased rollouts and multiple data centres/DR.
  • Establish and govern test automation frameworks for APIs, UI (web and mobile), and backend services, promoting high levels of automation in CI/CD pipelines.
  • Define test plans and standards for integration testing across modules and external systems (for example, government systems, telephony, GIS, messaging platforms, and databases).
  • Collaborate with DevOps and Infrastructure teams to align test environments, environment configuration, and data refresh strategies with deployment models, including active-active DC and DR.
  • Define non-functional testing strategies (for example, performance, load, stress, soak, failover, and DR testing) and ensure they are executed as part of major releases.
  • Set up and maintain standards for test data management, including anonymization or masking where needed, to ensure realistic and secure test datasets.
  • Provide leadership and guidance to QA and test teams, ensuring consistent application of test processes, tools, and best practices across projects.
  • Define and maintain a test governance model, including entry/exit criteria, defect severity/priority definitions, and release readiness criteria.
  • Collaborate with Security and DevSecOps teams to ensure security testing (for example, SAST/DAST, vulnerability scanning) is included in the overall test strategy and pipeline.
  • Support UAT and business testing by providing guidance on test scenarios, acceptance criteria, and tools for user-facing validation.
  • Contribute to continuous improvement of testing practices, tools, and metrics, using data-driven insights to enhance quality and speed of delivery.
  • Participate in incident reviews and post-release retrospectives to identify testing gaps and update strategies accordingly.

Preferred Skills

Technical Skills

  • Strong experience designing and implementing test automation frameworks for web UIs (for example, Selenium, Playwright, Cypress), APIs (for example, REST-assured, Postman/Newman, Karate), and backend services.
  • Solid understanding of testing strategies for microservices and distributed systems, including contract testing, integration testing, and end-to-end scenario testing.
  • Experience with performance and load testing tools (for example, JMeter, Gatling, Locust) to validate throughput, latency, and resource utilization under realistic and peak loads.
  • Familiarity with CI/CD tools (for example, Azure DevOps, Jenkins, GitLab CI) and integrating automated tests into pipelines as quality gates.
  • Understanding of testing in complex, on-premises environments that involve multiple application tiers, GIS services (for example, ArcGIS), databases (for example, Oracle), and message buses/streaming platforms (for example, Kafka).
  • Knowledge of test management tools (for example, Azure Test Plans, JIRA/Xray, Zephyr, or similar) for planning, execution, and traceability.
  • Good understanding of software quality principles, risk-based testing, and test design techniques (for example, boundary value analysis, equivalence partitioning, combinatorial testing).
  • Experience with service virtualization and mocking tools to simulate unavailable or third-party systems during integration testing.
  • Familiarity with test automation for desktop or rich-client applications where relevant.
  • Understanding of observability and logging tools (for example, ELK/EFK, APM solutions) and how they can be used to support testing, troubleshooting, and root cause analysis.
  • Knowledge of testing strategies for GIS applications (for example, validating map layers, geocoding accuracy, routing results, and real-time location updates).

Experience and Soft Skills

  • 8+ years of experience in software testing and quality engineering, with at least 3 - 4 years in a Test Architect or equivalent senior QA leadership role.
  • Proven experience defining and implementing test strategies for large-scale, mission-critical systems with strict uptime and performance SLAs.
  • Experience working in environments with multiple data centres and DR, including participation in failover and DR testing exercises.
  • Strong communication and collaboration skills, with the ability to work with architects, developers, DevOps, GIS, infrastructure, and business stakeholders.
  • Ability to document test strategies, test architectures, standards, and procedures clearly and concisely.

Experience

  • Prior involvement in modernization projects where legacy applications and UIs was gradually replaced with microservices and modern web front ends, with sustained test coverage across the transition.
  • Experience working in regulated or high-compliance environments, ensuring traceability of requirements to test cases, results, and defects for audit purposes.

Secondary Skills

Technical Skills and Experience

  • Exposure to SRE and reliability engineering concepts (for example, SLOs, SLIs, error budgets) and how testing can support reliability goals.
  • Experience with chaos engineering or resilience testing tools and practices.
  • Familiarity with model-based testing, property-based testing, or other advanced testing techniques.
  • Knowledge of test data generation tools and synthetic data strategies.

IT Pre-Sales Engineer

Company: PIT Solutions (P) Ltd Location: Remote (night shift) Closing Date: 23, Dec 2025 Job Published: 03, Dec 2025 Contact Email: careers@pitsolutions.com Website: http://www.pitsolutions.com Company Address: Module No. 209-N, 9th Floor, Yamuna, SEZ IT Building, Technopark Phase III, Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala, India, 695583

Position Overview

The IT Pre-Sales Engineer is responsible for supporting the sales cycle by providing technical expertise, solution design, and strategic guidance to prospective clients. This role bridges the gap between customer needs and technology capabilities, working closely with sales, product, and engineering teams to deliver compelling, accurate, and scalable solutions.

Key Responsibilities

  1. Technical Discovery & Client Engagement

    • Conduct client discovery sessions to understand business objectives, technical requirements, and current infrastructure.
    • Translate client needs into well-defined technical requirements.
    • Deliver technical presentations, demonstrations, and proof-of-concepts (POCs).

  2. Solution Architecture & Design

    • Develop technical proposals, solution diagrams, architecture documents, and bill of materials (BOM).
    • Design end-to-end IT solutions across areas such as cloud (AWS/Azure/GCP), networking, security, applications, SaaS platforms, and integrations.
    • Ensure solutions meet scalability, security, compliance, and performance standards.

  3. Sales Support & Enablement

    • Collaborate with the sales team to craft winning proposals, RFP responses, and pricing strategies.
    • Participate in pre-sales meetings, pitch sessions, and technical Q&A with customers.
    • Assist with the creation of sales tools: presentations, case studies, and competitive analyses.

  4. Proof-of-Concepts & Pilot Management

    • Lead POCs, pilot deployments, and product evaluations.
    • Configure demo environments to showcase capabilities tailored to client requirements.
    • Document outcomes, risks, and recommendations.

  5. Cross-Functional Collaboration

    • Work with product and engineering teams to validate technical feasibility and provide customer feedback.
    • Partner with customer success teams to ensure successful handoff post-sale.
    • Stay updated on product roadmaps, new features, and industry trends.

  6. Technical Expertise & Continuous Improvement

    • Maintain deep knowledge in relevant technology domains and emerging solutions.
    • Provide training to sales teams on technical aspects and competitive differentiators.
    • Contribute to internal knowledge bases and solution frameworks.

Qualifications Required

  • Bachelor's degree in computer science, Information Technology, Engineering, or related field.
  • 3–7 years of experience in pre-sales, solution engineering, or technical consulting.
  • Strong understanding of cloud computing, networking, security, APIs, and modern IT architectures.
  • Ability to communicate complex concepts to both technical and non-technical audiences.
  • Experience designing and presenting technical solutions to enterprise clients.

Preferred Qualifications

  • Certifications such as AWS Solutions Architect, Azure Solutions Architect Expert, CCNA/CCNP, CompTIA Security+, or equivalent.
  • Experience with SaaS platforms, DevOps tools, integration frameworks, and enterprise applications.
  • Background in RFP/RFI processes and proposal creation.
  • Experience with CRM or ticketing systems (Salesforce, HubSpot, Freshdesk, etc.).

Core Competencies

  • Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
  • Excellent verbal and written communication.
  • Customer-centric mindset with strong consultative skills.
  • Ability to work cross-functionally in fast-paced environments.
  • High ownership, self-driven, and detail-oriented.
